1)  
Fundamental Restoration  
We know that countless people have taken steps toward the unknown world of meaning. Thus, when the victorious foundation they have sought is established as a principle, they walk the path of restoration by following that principle. Therefore, you must understand that the path of restoration is a journey of seeking, and it is a path that walks based on the principles centered around that foundation they have found.  
Due to the fall, humanity has become the sons and daughters of Satan.  
The principles mean that if a grandfather has walked that path, his son or grandson cannot simply not walk it. The principles dictate that if the grandfather has walked that path, the son must walk it, and the grandson must also walk it. Whether a person lived a thousand years ago or will live a thousand years later, it is the same in walking the principles. That is the principle, you see.  
The principle does not manifest differently for different people; it appears in the same way regardless of whether one is a great person or a foolish person, regardless of gender or age, and it is pursued in the same form.  
This is something you must understand.  
So, is the path of the principle only for humans? No, God also meets humanity through the path of the principle. You must understand this. God seeks to walk the path of the principle, and humans must also strive to walk that path. Only through this dual path of the principle can there be a victorious reunion.  
Then, what is evil? Evil is what opposes walking the path of the principle. It is what prevents one from walking that path. It is placing obstacles in the way. Therefore, there is no forgiveness in the principles.  
How does the Republic of Korea govern its thirty million people as a sovereign nation? It governs with laws. What kind of laws? They are established based on the constitution and detailed regulations. Similarly, everything has its core.  
Looking at the path of restoration, we see that the ancestors of humanity made mistakes. What was the first mistake? They did not believe. They lost their faith. And what was lost due to this lack of belief? They lost their essence, their reality. They lost the body that could receive God's love. In other words, those who have fallen to the earth have become the descendants of disbelief. Thus, they have become beings with essence but have no relation to God. That essence has become the enemy of God, Satan, or the essence of God's enemy.  
What else did they lose? They lost the love that God intended to bind them with ideals. This is the three major conditions. You must understand this.  
First, disbelief began, then our bodies became the bodies of Satan, and our love became the love that breeds Satan's descendants. This is the problem.  
So, what happened because of disbelief, the loss of essence, and the loss of love? We were born through a different lineage. Our father has changed.  
When viewed this way, what was the final result of the fall? Of course, we stood in opposition to God's will and became sinful people who could not stand before heaven. As a result of committing sin, what happened? Those who should have been the sons and daughters of God became the sons and daughters of Satan.  
In other words, we should have honored our original father, but instead, we have taken Satan, whom we could not even imagine, as our father and inherited his bloodline, being born as the descendants of sinners. This is the problem.  
Disbelief became the root, allowing Satan to invade our bodies, and as a result of Satan's invasion, what did we become, connected through love centered on Satan? We became the offspring of Satan.  
Expectation of Faith and Reality for Restoration through Indemnity  
Now, we must restore this through indemnity, but how do we proceed with the restoration? This is the issue. You have learned about the 'expectation of faith' through the Principle book. What is the reason for establishing that expectation of faith? It is to rise to a position above the standard that Adam had when he believed in God. The expectation of faith is set up for that purpose. It is not anything else. Because Adam fell due to disbelief, we cannot return to our original position without having a faith that is greater than Adam's.  
Furthermore, we must rise to a position above the standard that Adam had regarding his knowledge of God. Adam fell in his youth, but we must become mature in faith. In this light, to establish the standard of 'expectation of faith,' everyone must be better than Adam. We cannot restore unless we rise to a position higher than that of our ancestors before the fall.  
Jesus came to this earth and said about the fallen people of this earth, "No one can come to the Father unless they love me more than anyone else." Here, "more than anyone else" means "better than our ancestor Adam."  
Everything is included in this statement.  
No matter how excellent something may be, unless one loves Jesus more than that, they cannot come before God.  
Moreover, Jesus said, "I am the way, the truth, and the life; no one comes to the Father except through me." What kind of way is that? It is not the way that has fallen and been lost. It is the way of restoration. This way has come about through Jesus, that is, through the Messiah. Right? "I am the way, the truth," which means he speaks of the true, and then "the life; no one comes to the Father except through me," which indicates that there is no indemnity. Shouldn't it be so? Anyone can be included in that. Even one's beloved mother, father, spouse, or children are included.  
In other words, a mature individual is centered around parents, spouse, and children. There are also neighbors and relatives, and a nation's king, but unless one loves Jesus more than anyone else, they cannot come before God.  
Then what was Adam's fall? If Adam had established a relationship of love in an absolutely undeniable position, it would have been absolute love. If that had happened, there would have been no need for the statement, "No one can come to the Father unless they love me." They would already be before the Father, having started from that position, and would not need to engage in the act of love again. However, humanity has fallen, which is why there is no way to return without rising above the position of the original sinner.  
Then what was the motive for the fall? Disbelief became the motive for the fall. Originally, humans were to overcome and dominate Satan, but by being in a position of disbelief, they came under Satan's dominion.  
So how should the expectation of faith be established? We must offer a standard of sacrifice that is better than Satan before God. What kind of sacrifice should we offer? We must offer a sacrifice that is better than Satan. This is why the act of offering sacrifices through Cain and Abel took place. However, Abel must be better than Cain. Right? Cain symbolizes the side of Satan. Therefore, Abel, who symbolizes the side of heaven, must be better than the standard of the side of Satan; otherwise, he cannot rise above the position of Adam, who saw the beginning of the side of Satan. Do you understand?  
Thus, to establish the expectation of faith, we must offer a sacrifice that is better than Cain's. Cain represents the side of Satan. Satan refers to the fallen archangel. Therefore, we must be higher than the standard of the motive from which Satan started. This is the principle.  
After establishing the expectation of faith, we must establish the expectation of reality. What is the expectation of reality? Humanity has been led away by Satan due to the fall. Therefore, we must retrieve the essence that was taken by Satan. To do this, we must overcome Satan. Thus, we must engage in the act of overcoming Satan.  
Because humanity has fallen, the condition of indemnity is necessary.  
In overcoming Satan, we must not center on individual conditions like "you and I." It must be "you, the representative of the world of Satan, and I, the representative of the world of heaven." Do you understand? It is not just the two of us standing together. They are two, but they represent the side of Satan and the side of heaven, respectively. A representative is not alone; they stand in the same position as that world. When I say I represent the Unification Church, I am one person, but I represent the entire Unification Church.  
In this way, Cain represented Satan, and Abel represented heaven, so Cain represents the entire world of Satan, and Abel represents the entire world of heaven. You must always think this way. Abel always represents the entire world of heaven.  
Because Abel represents the entire world of heaven, he is the resurrection body of Abraham, the resurrection body of Noah, and likewise the representative of Abraham, Jacob, Moses, and Jesus. This is how you should view it.  
Then what does it mean to represent evil? It means being the representative of Cain, the representative of the people who disbelieved in Noah's time, and the representative of the nations that opposed Abraham. It also means being the representative of all those who opposed Jacob, just like the Egyptians before Moses and the entire Roman Empire before Jesus.  
Thus, even though a person is one, in content, it must be universal. It must be universal. You must understand this.  
Did Satan only take Adam when he led him away? The family, tribe, nation, world, and hopes that were within Adam's ideals were all led away because Adam was taken. Is that not so? Therefore, within Adam, there is the world. Then what is Abel? He is the substitute for Adam. What is Cain? He is the representative of the world of Satan.  
What is the restoration of reality? It is the act of Adam, who was overcome by Satan, overcoming Satan in return. It is not about overcoming as a flat individual but about overcoming as a representative of the entire dimension. Therefore, that relationship is not an ordinary individual-to-individual relationship. Do you understand?  
Abel represents heaven, and Cain represents the earth. They represent the whole. You must understand this. Because Adam was overcome by Satan and led away, in today's age of restoration, Abel, who represents the side of heaven, must overcome Cain, who represents the side of Satan. This is the act of restoring Satan back to the archangel who became a servant from the original position of being God's son. This is the restoration of reality. This is how it works. When this restoration of reality occurs, we can finally meet the motivation to receive God's love without conflict from here. Do you understand?  
Then, shouldn't the restored Adam himself receive love directly from God? In other words, if fallen humanity has restored reality, shouldn't that restored position simply receive God's love? You might think so, but that cannot happen. Why?  
Where did we start from? We started from evil. This is how it is. Fallen humanity does not start from goodness, does not start from God, but starts from evil.  
Therefore, we, who started from evil, need conditions of indemnity. If we had started from goodness, we would not need conditions of indemnity. Because we started from evil, those who started from here cannot return without establishing conditions of indemnity. There are various expectations of faith and reality, but even if we have established the expectation of reality, it is still based on the fallen world, not on heaven. According to the original principled standard, from what standard should humanity start? Humanity must start from God.  
When God created humanity, humanity started from God's side, but due to the fall, the new start began from Satan. Is that not so? Therefore, all ideal starts and all hopes that humanity desires do not start from God. They start from Satan. Thus, humanity, which started from Satan, is not in a position where the starting point is heaven. It is different. Do you understand? Therefore, the position in which we find ourselves still has conditions of indemnity remaining. This is how it is.  
Because of the fall, we must be grafted onto the Messiah.  
Therefore, without inheriting the position from which we can be restored, starting from God, we cannot occupy the original position based on the principle and cannot meet the original God of the principle. Thus, without establishing a subject that has not deviated from God and has started from God, we have no way to go. This is how it is.  
Then what is this one subject? It is the Messiah. To restore the path, the Messiah is needed. Do you understand? This is why the 'expectation for the Messiah' is necessary. Do you understand what I mean? You must clearly understand this when you look at the Principle book.
Then what kind of position should the representative's seat be here? (Speaking while writing on the board) There is still a way for Satan to accuse. Even though the substantial expectation has been restored, the belief in losing has been lost, the substance has been lost, and then love has been lost, which is why there are still conditions of indemnity that need to be fulfilled to achieve the purpose of love. This is how it is. That is why, centered on the original owner, there is still no relationship established.

For example, what kind of seat is this? (Speaking while writing on the board) Because of the fall, what should have become a true persimmon tree has become a wild persimmon tree. What kind of persimmon tree has it become? It has become a wild persimmon tree. When you look at the wild persimmon, it is only food for the magpies. There is something called a "go-youm" (wild persimmon), right? This wild persimmon tree, just standing there as a wild persimmon tree, is of no use anywhere. However, if this wild persimmon tree, how should I say it, is grafted, there is a way for the new true persimmon fruit to be borne. What is that way? It is the game of grafting. Do you understand what I mean? It is the game of grafting.

If you cut the wild persimmon tree and graft a true persimmon tree onto it, will this wild persimmon tree remain a wild persimmon tree, or will it become a true persimmon tree? "It becomes a true persimmon tree." It becomes a true persimmon tree. Therefore, within the realm of Satan, in other words, in the world of wild persimmons, there is a need for just one true persimmon tree. The day that this one true persimmon tree appears, the wild persimmon field can be turned into a true persimmon field. Will that happen just by leaving it alone? It is restored through indemnity. Do you understand? Therefore, if the wrong start is corrected through indemnity, can a person who was to become a wild persimmon tree become a true persimmon tree or not? "Yes." It can.

So who is the owner of this wild persimmon field? Is it God or Satan? Without a doubt, Satan is the owner. Since the start was from Satan, the result is bound to be on Satan's side, so without a doubt, Satan is the owner. Then can God manage this wild persimmon field, which is owned by Satan, at will? Is it possible or not? "It is not possible." It is not possible. If this world were a wild persimmon field that God could manage, He could plant a true persimmon tree there, and once it sprouts and grows, He could cut down the wild persimmons at will and graft whenever He wanted. Isn't that right? However, it is not a wild persimmon field that God can manage; who manages it? It is Satan. Who has emerged as the absolute owner who can manage it? It is Satan.

However, God can argue from a principled standpoint against Satan, saying, "Hey, you! Although a person was born in the form of a wild persimmon tree, isn't the essence of a person originally something that belonged to me?" In that case, Satan cannot say, "No." He must say, "Yes, that is correct. From a principled standpoint, it is a principle that humans should love you more than they love me, so in order to be a person who can take what you need, they must be able to love you more than they love me; otherwise, there is no one who can return to you." That is principled. Isn't that right?

In this way, Satan develops arguments and fights against God from a principled standpoint. Saying, "There is no way to return without believing in you more than I believe in myself," is principled. Isn't that right? And also, "In the global battlefield, unless someone fights against me and defeats me, there is no one who can return to you," is all principled. Isn't that right? Therefore, Satan argues that "unless you believe in God more than you believe in me, there is no way to separate from the wild persimmon field." That is what Satan claims.

Thus, even those in the wild persimmon field can separate from it when they come to have absolute faith in God. This is how it works.

In order for the ideal world to come, there is faith, faith. And religious people live a life of faith. What kind of life do they live? A life of believing. Then, religious people must fight. Who do they have to fight? It is not a fight among brothers. They must fight against Satan. How does Satan appear? Whenever someone tries to do something new and good, Satan is bound to appear. When trying to do good, both Satan and God appear. Therefore, you are in a position between good and evil. Isn't that right?

Thus, you must stand in a position where you can subdue evil and leave good, so that evil can automatically comply. To put it in principled terms, this is the completion of the substantial expectation. To achieve this, you must fight and win against Satan.

Then what should you do after defeating Satan? Since you have defeated Satan, you must receive a reward. What kind of reward? In the world, they give awards and money as prizes, but it is not such trivial rewards. It is a reward, but what kind of reward? It is the love of God, which is the only one. Isn't that amazing? That is the ideal type that humanity seeks.

So, through whom do we receive love? Originally, God's love is received through parents. This is how it works. Originally, for us humans to be born and connect with God's love, it must be through parents. Otherwise, there is no way to receive love.

Therefore, today, fallen humans are seeking what? They are seeking the Messiah.

Who is the Messiah? He is the one who comes to give us rebirth as parents. This is how it works. That is why Christianity speaks of resurrection and so on.

Then, to give rebirth, through what does He give rebirth? It is not through life that He gives rebirth. It is through love that He gives rebirth.

Where does that love start? Parents are parents centered on the relationship between father and son, but who is the original subject of love? The original subject of love is God. If God represents heaven as the subject of love, then Adam represents the subject of love on earth.

From this perspective, the father is the subject of love. Do you understand? Because the father is the subject of love, the mother, who is the counterpart to that subject father, must come forth. Isn't that right? This is what Christianity has yet to find—the position of the father and mother. The way to find that is decisively taught through the concept of the bride and groom. Do you understand?

What is the groom? It refers to the father, and what about the bride? It refers to the mother. Also, heaven symbolizes the man, and earth symbolizes the woman. That is why Jesus, who came to this earth, ascended to heaven. Therefore, just as man and woman become one, heaven and earth must become one for the ideal to unfold here. Thus, no matter how hard humans try, the ideal world will not come with just the people of the human world. It must be a world centered on heaven, with heaven as the subject and earth as the object, before the ideal world can come.

Among the many people seeking the ideal world, who is a representative person? What kind of person is an ideal person? It is those who prioritize "Godism" in their lives and strive to align their entire lives with it. They are the ideal representatives of this earth. What do humans call such ideal representatives? They call them saints. You understand, right?

Those ideal representatives did not center on humanity absolutely; they centered on God absolutely. Therefore, when we look at the four great saints left in history, what kind of people were they? They were undoubtedly people who loved God the most and were the most representative antiques of what God desired and envisioned. Do you understand? Don't feel bad when I call them antiques. I say this to leave an impression on you.

From a worldly perspective, they may seem like foolish people. Why? Because they were people who had no personal claims. 

Look at Jesus. Jesus also said, "Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. But let your will be done, not mine." He did not say, "Let my will be done, and let your will be done." In that, does Jesus have a will or not? Jesus also has a will. He desires not to die, but God wants him to die. So, isn't there a conflict? There is a conflict. That is why he is a person without a personal will. He does not want to die, but if told to die, he must say, "Yes." Who does he say "yes" for? He says "yes" for God. 

When we observe this fact, saints were not people who lived claiming themselves. Who did they claim? They claimed God. This is the difference. Also, when we look at these four great saints, they all became the leaders of religions, right? Isn't that right? Why is that?

Today, young people shake their heads and dislike the word "religion." People say that religion is what the weak believe in, but aren't the representatives who carry the banner of being global saints all people who absolutely revere God? Are they believers or not? "They are believers." 

The man in the brown jacket, is he a believer or not? What is he? "……." Look over there! Why is he acting like that? (Laughter) What is it? No matter how loudly he shouts, he is just blinking his eyes…. (Laughter) What has he done? What has he done while sitting there? What does that person prove? He proves that he was dozing off! (Laughter) It is certain. The results are bound to appear as they began.

Now, is a saint a good person or a foolish person? "He is a good person." From a human perspective? "He is a foolish person." He is a foolish person, but from God's perspective? "He is a good person." He is a good person. You must understand this. Therefore, history is all organized through the cultural realm of religion, receiving the teachings of the saints.

What is the foundation of the Constitution of the Republic of Korea? Do you think it was established by saying, "Ah, I am a citizen of the Republic of Korea, so I must act according to my claims"? No, it is not. The essence of the saint's teachings was extracted and organized into the Constitution of the Republic of Korea and the constitutions of various countries around the world. Ultimately, the world is organized according to the will of the saints. Is that wrong or right? "It is right." Many people, despite clearly seeing this, are crazy about disliking religion. So, is a person who opposes religion a good person or a crazy person? "A crazy person." A crazy person? Why call them a person? They are crazy people. Do you understand? "Yes."

In the end, "I thought the saint was good, but he is a foolish person, and because the one he loves is good, he is blessed through that and becomes great." This is how it works. Our Unification Church members are also quite foolish. They are quite foolish, but what do Unification Church members want to do? Do they want to be below the saints? If you turn the foolishness upside down, what does it become? It becomes greatness. So, let’s turn it upside down.

Did the saints fulfill their will or not? They did not fulfill it. Confucius did not fulfill it, nor did Buddha, and no one else fulfilled it either. Yet the one who was said to have run the best was Jesus, but even Jesus did not fulfill his will.

So what do the Unification Church members today want to do? They want to perform the work of restoration for Jesus. They want to perform the work of restoration for Jesus, but can they do that if they are worse than Jesus? For example, if I owe ten million won and I only have ten million won, after paying off that debt, is there anything left? No, there is not. I would have to borrow again. Is that right or not? If that happens, is there anything they can claim? If they pay off the debt and still have nothing left, can they say, "I am better than you"? No, they cannot. They must have more than the person they borrowed from to be able to speak confidently. Isn't that right? 

In the same way, if you are worse than the saints or if you can only do what they could not do through indemnity and restoration, is there anything left for you? Do you want to live by receiving from them or by giving to them? "I want to live by giving." You want to live by giving, right? So, can you perform the restoration for them if you are worse than the saints? "No, I cannot." If you say you will perform the restoration for them while being worse than the saints, Satan will come to the top and chase you away, saying, "Hey! What are you trying to do? Get out of here!" Then you would be too ashamed to show your face and would run away. This must not happen.

Therefore, are the Unification Church members worse than the saints? "No." Really? Then you should say "Jesus" to Jesus, right? "Jesus, my friend!" Should you say that? (Laughter) In the past, they called Jesus "Lord," but now Jesus…. You see, a teacher is always a teacher, right? If a primary school teacher has a student who becomes a high school teacher, they must also call that person "teacher." Is that so or not? If the primary school teacher says, "I am the teacher, and the high school teacher is useless," they will always remain a primary school teacher and will struggle. If their student becomes a high school teacher, they must call them "teacher." Isn't that right?

The same goes for the Unification Church. In the Unification Church, they thought that Teacher Moon was the best…. If the teacher tries to raise you to be worse than Teacher Moon, that is a failure in education. Is that a good thing or a bad thing? "It is a bad thing." It is a bad thing, right? Therefore, Unification Church members must be better than the teacher. Only then will their family prosper, and their country will prosper.

When looking at a family, if the parents give birth to and raise their children, and if the children are absolutely worse than the parents, will that family prosper or perish? "It will perish." It will perish.
Therefore, if the world becomes one that wishes to live under the teachings of the saints indefinitely, it will result in a world where the ideal world cannot come to fruition, centered around the ideals led by the saints that have not been realized. Thus, it is an undeniable fact that a better saint than the saints of old must emerge.

So, what kind of group are the Unification Church followers? They are a group that has appeared to become better people than the saints. When they go to the spirit world, won't Jesus, Confucius, Buddha, and Muhammad boast to each other, saying, "I have many followers"? Jesus will say, "Look at those Christian believers who believe in me. They have followed me and even sacrificed their lives for me." Buddha might say, "Ah! This Eastern Buddhism, which has a longer history than yours, started in India, and I take pride in the fact that only Eastern people believe in it." They can boast in their own ways. Can there be unity among the saints if they boast about themselves like this? Can religions unite? "No, they cannot."

Currently, Christianity claims it will unify the world centered around Jesus, Buddhism claims it is the best in its own way, and Confucianism claims it is the best in its own way. Can there be unity when each claims to be the best? Therefore, when compared, one must be better than Jesus. Is that right? One must be better than Confucius and better than Buddha. Only when something better rises to the top can there be no complaints; but when something lesser rises to the top, what happens? Are there complaints in the world or not? "There are complaints."

In the world, if the worst student becomes the class president, do people listen to him? "What is that guy! If you are the class president, that's all there is to it, you fool!" Even if they say that, they just roll their eyes. The authority of the class president does not stand. However, if someone studies well and confidently becomes the class president, even if he is as small as a pea, when he says, "Hey, listen," it may feel unpleasant, but they will listen. (Laughter) This shows that if one is not better than others, they cannot dominate.

Unification Church members must become better than Jesus. Do you want to unify religions today? What is the Unification Church? What are we trying to unify? Are we trying to unify religions? Are we just trying to unify Christianity? If you have the audacity to say you want to unify all religions, can a group that is worse than Jesus unify religions? Can a group that is worse than Buddha unify religions?

Look at this. If you go to a child and say, "Hey, let's trade yours for mine!" and that child, not knowing better, agrees to trade, what happens when they look at what they got and realize they can't have it? "Oh no!" (Laughter) Will they cry or not? "They will cry." They will cry. But if they look at it and think, "Oh, this is nice," then they will be happy. "Hooray!" Everything in the world works this way. Those who find joy in what is lesser are crazy. It is normal to find joy in what is good and better. Is that right? This is how it is. Therefore, even when trying to unify religions, those who claim to do so while being worse than the saints of the past are foolish.

Thus, when the Unification Church first emerged, it must have content that is better than Jesus. This is obvious. Is that right? It means that it has brought something different from what Buddha or Confucius hoped for. When compared to them, can unity occur if it is worse than them? "No, it cannot." Therefore, the emergence of the Unification Church in the world concludes that there must be something greater behind it.

For this reason, Unification Church members must at least be a hair's breadth better than the saints; being lesser will not accomplish anything. "Wow, listening to this sounds great, it feels good..." they may say, but the truth is the problem. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." So, do you say you are better than Jesus? "Yes, we are better." (Laughter) Are you better than Jesus? "Yes." You are better than Jesus when it comes to eating! When it comes to eating... (Laughter) You are better than Jesus when it comes to sleeping, playing, and thinking about your own matters. There are many things you are better at. (Laughter) However, no matter how much better you are at those things, are they useful? "No, they are not." They are of no use. They are useless. No matter how much you pile them up like a mountain or spread them out like the Pacific Ocean, they will not be of any use. This is how it is.

So, in what way must you be better than Jesus? You must be exceedingly better in serving God. When Jesus prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane, "Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as you will," if someone can think, "Jesus prayed incorrectly. He needs to be educated," then that person is better than Jesus? "Yes, they are better." If someone can say, "Jesus, why did you pray like that in the Garden of Gethsemane?" then they are not worse than Jesus? "No, they are not."

The reason I ask this insistently is that you might doze off. I have to speak in a question-and-answer format so you won't doze off.

Jesus said, "Not as I will, but as you will," but there are already two wills here. Do you understand?

So, centered around our Unification Church, is your will and the teacher's will two or one? Is it one? "Yes." Is it two or one? "It is one." When the teacher says, "Hey! Don't go back today; let's live here," if you respond, "Why? If I don't go back to my husband, it will be a big deal; why should I live here?" then are the teacher's will and your will the same or different? "They are different." They are different.

Therefore, the will of Jesus, who said, "Not as I will, but as you will," is different from God's will, right? So, from the beginning, are they one or not? They are not one. This means that it is not the way to pray. Where is my will, and where is God's will? God's will is my will. "Because your will is this way, I am trying to follow that will. The Character of the Teacher
You all need to know this. Good and evil occupy different places. They are on different paths. You need to understand that. Where do good and bad people diverge? Those who move for themselves ultimately use others, while those who move for others are serving others. That’s how it works.

The Unification Church’s Teacher has fought until now without thinking of himself. Even when I wear clothes, I don’t wear them for myself. There are good clothes. When I wear good clothes, others might show off, but for some reason, I can’t hold my head up. The Teacher has a nice Lincoln car. It’s a world-famous car. That’s how differently I think.

Also, if someone offers to elevate me for no reason, I would rather die than accept it. There are people who like to be praised for no reason, right? Even if I have results, if I think I’m worth a certain score and someone thinks higher of me, I feel embarrassed. I possess that kind of heart. When I see that, I don’t think I’m a bad person. (laughter)

In the past, my family was well-off in the neighborhood. When friends who were starving brought lunch boxes of millet or barley rice, I couldn’t eat my rice just by looking at them. I could eat if I exchanged it… When friends’ parents were sick and couldn’t afford to go to the hospital, I would go to their parents, shedding tears, asking for money to send them to the hospital. “Will you give it or not?” If they didn’t give it, I would declare to my parents, “I have something to spend money on, I’ll sell some goods, so please understand.” That’s something I can’t forget. I was about eleven years old then, about the age of Hyojin now. Back then, I declared to my father that I would help someone by selling a bag of rice. I still remember carrying a bag of rice secretly and walking twenty miles. I had to have a rope or something to carry it, but I just carried it. My heart was pounding (laughter), and my chest was racing, I was gasping countless times. I can’t forget that. It will never be forgotten in my lifetime. All of that put me in a position to go for the purpose.

Interestingly, our Hyojin, when her friend is wronged and gets scolded by her father, cries and says, “Dad, I’m going to someone’s house.” When I see her crying, I wonder how she resembles me so much… (laughter) And our Gukjin baby, when his parents come back from the countryside after about five months, what does the baby know? Systematization Plan for a Global Economic Organization

However, in the future, while the number of advanced countries will continue to increase, the sales market will be limited. Right? The sales market does not expand as the number of advanced countries increases. The sales market is fixed, but as the number of advanced countries increases, an era of competition among advanced countries will come. They are already competing, right? If several countries compete based on that one sales channel, the production prices will gradually decrease. This means that there will be a stage where producers will not make any profits. That time is coming.
If they start to fight among themselves, some of the advanced countries will fail. Therefore, there will inevitably come a time when advanced countries will collectively produce and distribute common benefits to developing countries. Do you understand what I mean? Such an era is bound to come. Until now, only the producing countries among advanced countries have benefited, which has caused discomfort for developing countries. In the future, in the global economic utilization, if only a few advanced countries produce, they can meet the global consumption needs. Other countries will not need to establish production factories. When advanced countries collectively form a club and distribute benefits to developing countries, it will be possible for the entire world to utilize each other through the production of just a few countries.
Then, which group will be able to control the global economic sphere? Neither advanced nor developing countries. It will be a group or country that has a global sales organization that can control the global economic sphere. This is the conclusion that emerges. Do you understand? <Words> In our Unification Church, there is a special day of celebration that no other religious organization has. That day, as you all know, is Parents' Day, Children's Day, Day of All Things, and God's Day. This order of commemorative days has been established in our church.

The background of the days celebrated in the Unification Church and their establishment
In the world, individuals have commemorative days in their own lives. Families also have commemorative days. And nations have their own days of celebration that they take pride in.

However, from God's perspective, He has never had a day to celebrate any individual. Moreover, there has never been a day to celebrate families, tribes, nations, or any true meaning of celebration. Historically, there have been days that the nation of Israel could commemorate, but those days could not fulfill God's wishes. While there may have been days to celebrate from a hopeful perspective, there has never been a day when heaven and earth could unite in celebration.

The day Jesus was born may have been a day that God could celebrate, but… if Jesus had come to this earth and fulfilled the original mission sent by God, that is, if He had completed the responsibilities He had to fulfill on earth and had a day of celebration for victory and glory, then the day Jesus was born would have indeed been a day more worthy of celebration than any other day centered on an individual in the world.

Humanity has commemorated the day of Jesus' birth as a day of celebration, but from God's position, who looks upon the glory, that day cannot be a day of joy. Behind the celebration of the born Jesus lies the heart of God, who cannot help but think of the dead Jesus.

From this perspective, our Unification Church declared Parents' Day. That is, in 1960, we declared Parents' Day and also declared Children's Day. Following that, we declared the Day of All Things. These days of Parents' Day, Children's Day, and Day of All Things are days established not only within the limited context of the Unification Church but are known to be declared from a broader perspective. The declaration of these days was made in light of a historical mission.

When we look at human history, what is the historical wish? It is for the original standard, the original starting point, where humans did not fall, to manifest on this earth. This is the historical wish. It has been the hope of countless prophets who have walked the path of death before that wish. The time when that wish can bear fruit is Parents' Day, Children's Day, Day of All Things, and furthermore, God's Day. These days become a day when God can finally rejoice after creating heaven and earth. The day God can rejoice is also the day Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity, can rejoice. Moreover, it is the day that all things, which must be under the dominion of Adam and Eve, can rejoice. In other words, that day becomes the day of God's joy, the day of the joy of the ancestors of humanity, and furthermore, the day when all things existing on earth can rejoice. If this had been the case, we would have indeed seen the beginning of a world of freedom and peace without lamentation. This was the ideal of creation.

Current Moment
Are most of you church leaders here? Please raise your hands if you are a church leader. Put them down. And then the evangelism team members. Almost no hands are raised. I will speak on the topic of "Current Moment."

Importance of Time
The question of what time it is for our Unification Church is a significant issue in everyone's faith life. If we fail to accurately capture the present, we cannot fulfill the historical mission woven from the past.

We know that in any era, providence has been passed down from ancestors. For example, when we consider Noah, he inherited what Abel failed and was born at a time that matched a period of 1,600 years. Thus, by appropriately completing the circumstances that needed to be fulfilled at that time and offering them before Heaven, the will is accomplished.

That is why it is often said that no matter how much of a hero one is, if they do not catch the right time, they cannot succeed as a hero. Similarly, on June 13, 1972 (Tuesday), at Gwangju Church.

Time is very important. If one miscalculates the time, everything becomes futile.

When we look at a day, it is divided into morning, noon, evening, and night. Although these seem the same, they change differently every moment. There are times in the transition from morning to noon when we cannot tell if it is morning or noon. Similarly, there are moments in the transition from noon to evening when we cannot distinguish whether it is still noon or has become evening. The same goes for night. There are crossroads where changes occur.

The changing times can be unnoticed if we are not careful. Right? We may not realize when the change is happening.

Even when we observe the four seasons, the days that transition from spring to summer change in an instant, and we may not recognize it, saying, "Ah! Spring is passing, and now it is summer." Although it is a simple matter, it is difficult for anyone to recognize. The same applies to the transition from summer to autumn and from autumn to winter.

Likewise, when we look at a person's life, it goes through childhood, youth, adulthood, and old age. However, when this transition occurs, no one remembers to say, "Ah, now childhood is ending, and we are moving into youth." Just like racehorses at the starting line, no one feels the seriousness of that moment.

Our lives also make it difficult to catch the moment of transition. It is rare for someone to accurately recognize the time and say, "This is the moment," and then joyfully embrace the new era from that moment of "Go!" declaring, "I am entering a new youth from this time." 

The fate of our Republic of Korea is the same. Even if the national fortune has been poor until now, we do not know when a good fortune will come after the bad one passes. The same applies to each of you.

Although we may be in a difficult position now, if we can overcome this difficulty, a path to true happiness and blessings will appear. If we can find that moment when the path opens up and embrace it, we can bring about a fortunate destiny. However, if we miss that moment, we may lose the opportunity for blessings. You must understand this.

Prepared for the Right Time: Mary and Joseph
For example, looking at Mary during the time of Jesus, when the angel appeared to her and said, "You will conceive the Son of God," if Mary had had anything to assert about herself, would it have been fulfilled? If Mary had said, "Ah! I am like this and that, so it cannot be," would it have been accomplished? God cannot forcibly make her conceive Jesus just because she says it cannot be.

So, what kind of woman was Mary? She was someone who had a keen understanding and prepared herself to accurately receive the time. "God must exist, and His will will surely be revealed through the nation of Israel, either through a man or a woman. Even if there are many people in Israel, the starting point for connecting the will among the people is not through all of them at once, but through one man or one woman. If a man understands the will and conveys it to a woman, that first woman to receive it will be one person." This is how we should view Mary.

Therefore, it does not matter who conveys the message, whether they are disabled, elderly, or a baby. The issue is not who conveys it but the timing of the long-awaited moment. Whether it is conveyed by a person or through some spiritual being or angel, the important thing is the significance of that moment, where one can offer everything to it. When one can invest everything into that one point, they can accurately capture the heavenly fortune that comes.

Similarly, Mary devoted her entire being to the angel's words, aligning herself completely with that moment. No matter how much effort Mary had put in or how much she had longed for it, if the timing had been off, everything would have been in vain. Is that not true? Do you understand? "Yes."

Joseph was the same. The angel appeared to him in a dream and said, "Take Mary." It was not a matter of waking up and being forced to decide, "Hey, if you don't take Mary, you're in trouble. Are you going to take her or not?" In the dream, the angel said, "Do not be afraid to take Mary." There are all kinds of dreams, including nonsense ones, and if it were just a dream, it would be unbelievable.

However, for Joseph, the command to take Mary was a serious matter that affected everything in his life, and he was able to overcome it.

From this, we see that Joseph was a good man. He thought, "God must have done something good through a man in Israel, regardless of the means." He valued that message more than the nation of Israel. Therefore, he removed all favorable conditions that a man could consider and resolved to take a risk and overcome everything, which allowed for the circumstances that led to Jesus' birth.

Heavenly fortune comes in the smallest moments
Historical events, global matters, or the origins of revolutions cannot be accomplished by mobilizing an entire nation at once. It begins from something that seems extremely insignificant, such as one person, and if that moment is missed, the fate of the entire nation can be lost. The fate of a single individual is even more so.

When heavenly fortune that can determine the life and death of heaven and earth comes, whether one accepts it or not does not happen in a place where everyone can see it. It is not known whether one knows or not, but it is centered around a specific man or woman who is connected. Do you understand? "Yes."

For example, let’s say the king is disguised as an inspector traveling the country. He may appear shabby and insignificant. If he goes to a house late in the evening and asks for a place to sleep, but someone is waiting for a precious guest, even if their situation is difficult, they will prepare for the unexpected guest, thinking, "Perhaps this person is a precious guest." They will put in effort before he even speaks. However, if they think, "If a guest comes, fine, if not, that's okay. I don't want the trouble of a guest," they might end up treating the guest poorly and sending him away. If they welcome the guest well, they could receive blessings beyond measure, but if they fail to do so, they could end up unfortunate. Thus, the fortunes of the world are influenced by those who are unaware.

Sometimes, this is conveyed through words, sometimes through writing. Moreover, in the workings of heaven, it can be conveyed through dreams or revelations. Furthermore, at times, when one is walking down a path, if sparrows are chirping and dancing on a wall, it may indicate that they are pleased with that person. Even though it seems unrelated, there are moments when things align perfectly because of that. There are hints that teach us. Through indirect forms, even objects that cannot be thought of as subjects can accurately indicate that fact and let us know. This is how hints can teach us something.

If someone seriously thinks that everything connected to them happens due to relationships, then the sparrows chirping will surely teach them something. When this happens, it all becomes a secret.

Also, if the wind blows and leaves pass from left to right... if there is a fork in the road... one might feel, "I am now stepping onto the public path of heaven, and the wind is guiding me." Heaven teaches its fortune not only through people but also through all things that serve as examples. Therefore, those who seek that path, who practice the way, or who work for the will, live a life of seeking. It is natural for those who diligently align their lives with that search to be called and chosen for the gifts of the will. Do you understand? "Yes."

This gathering is the same. There may be someone here for the first time in the Unification Church. Someone may have encouraged them to come to this gathering. However, it is currently the season for rice planting. In Jeollanam-do, barley harvesting is in full swing, and one might think, "If I miss this opportunity today, I don't know when I will have it again." So, they might think, "Seeing how focused you are, I should go, but... I promised to go, and I want to go, but the barley threshing is a problem. If I want to plant rice, I need to prepare the seedbed and the field for transplanting, and I wish it had been a few days ago, but today is not possible." Then they might retreat slightly. However, this is not just about that person's life; it is about the path that has been paved by good ancestors, leading them to a moment where they can meet and intersect.

Countless ancestors have come together, standing on the side of goodness, and at the corner where heaven's command exists, there is a moment that can only be met. If one misses that moment, the achievements of a thousand years of good ancestors can be shattered. Do you understand? "Yes."

Perception of God in daily life as a factor of our existence
Everyone, when we say "love," it is a vague term. Love cannot be understood alone or through words. Perceive God's heart from a three-dimensional perspective
Saying "God exists, God exists" is not just words. When viewed through principles centered on the subject-object relationship, it is not a position that God must inevitably exist; rather, God existed before I did, before I thought, and is the heaven that governs all my senses and my entirety. Recognizing this is the most important issue. 

Isn't knowing and recognizing the principle? It is not that we know and recognize; rather, we are meant to recognize and then know. When we feel cold, we do not just know it; we feel it and then know it. Similarly, if God exists, you must feel that God exists. You must feel it at the cellular level. That level is the issue. In other words, the question is how we can establish a perceptual position.

When considering in what environment this is recognized, you do not wish for it to happen only during mystical prayers or prayer times, do you? Everything I hear and say must be three-dimensional, not flat. Religion does not start from thought. Religion begins from perception. When you watch a movie, you must understand that thrilling scenes are approaching us. 

Therefore, we need a better step, a better resolution and action. We must be in a position where today can be better than yesterday. To do this, it cannot be just me. It must be more like God, more like heaven... 

If you have shed tears for your country, you must shed even more at this time, and if you have devoted your heart, you must devote even more during this period. You must hold onto heaven and become one with heaven. You must understand this. 

When Moses failed to fulfill his responsibilities and passed the mission to Joshua and Caleb to send them before the seven nations of Canaan for the new second Israel, heaven told Joshua and Caleb, "Be strong and courageous. I am with you, so be strong and courageous. Trust in heaven and be strong and courageous." Heaven is coming forth with the belief that as much as you believe, I believe in you. Since the command is difficult, the heaven behind that command stands with the determination, belief, and responsibility to overcome difficulties.
Yes? I am facing that responsibility. The problem lies here.  
The issue is how to rediscover my shining self today, as I ignite my belief that can be stronger, with the goal set for the remaining six months in front of the envisioned belief and initiate new actions. This is undoubtedly a historical and important question. You must understand this.  
To do so, you must draw closer to heaven. When you shed tears, let them flow from a deeper place, embracing the nation and appealing, embracing the world and appealing, with a heart longing for the will of heaven, you must become someone who can appeal to be sent to take responsibility on behalf of heaven. You are to become one with heaven.  
Next, you must have the belief of a historical leader who will not yield to anyone in the historical age on behalf of history. I believe the problem lies here. Only by discovering the self that realizes there is no one else to take on the historical responsibility if I do not unite with heaven can we illuminate the more meaningful present standards, and surely, the foundation for a new tomorrow will be formed.  
Now is the time to reach the highest speed.  
Therefore, when recalling the past that was loyal to the cause, you should not only look back and boast about that past self but also reflect on the current self that has become inferior to then. You must surpass the standards you worked hard to achieve back then.  
At that time, I worked hard alone, but as time has passed, I now have a wife and perhaps children, right? I must show and stimulate something beyond the value of my loyal past in front of my wife. And I must let my children know this. Furthermore, I must strengthen the horizontal connections centered around my family. Thus, in front of families... You must have the resolve that you cannot go on like this, and when you meet, hold each other's hands and do not miss this time, and when you press your foreheads together to speak, you must respect each other.  
Today, we have many issues to reflect on anew. When we meet, we are only talking about trivial matters. There are too many captains. We must eliminate this. Standing in deep silence, meditating on the inner connection with heaven, lamenting the inadequate as a practical self, we must realize that we cannot neglect our mission as pioneers of ourselves moment by moment.  
We must not speak with our mouths and utter evil words. When we meet and open our mouths, we must make a new pledge while holding hands. "We must pioneer tomorrow. Let’s overcome today." If we do not horizontally expand such activities and movements, we cannot create such an environment or atmosphere.  
Until now, we have lived somewhat passively... You must understand that living passively cannot bring historical victory before us.  
In front of the innovative belief that eliminates habitual evils, we must establish a foundation for a new self-awareness, revealing a strong, subjectively empowered self, and when we collide with heaven, the history of new creation begins from here. You must understand that whenever this has happened, a new history of creation has emerged.  
That is why you must break the habitual tendencies and establish a new meaningful, subjective inner connection, becoming both a creator and a sacrifice in overcoming the environment as a pioneering subject.  
Isn't it time to feel this?  
Today exists for tomorrow. Tomorrow is not here to bring me sorrow but to bring glory and victory that can shine brighter. Therefore, since that victory must be complete, we must pursue today's completeness. That completeness must not be formed solely by me but must be recognized as complete by heaven. That is why we must stand in a position where we can pursue perfection in unity with heaven and invest our whole heart and effort. Individuals must be invested, families must be invested, nations must be invested, and the state must be invested. The whole that is invested can be resurrected. You must understand this.  
An individual cannot act arbitrarily. A person who does not have a better present in the past and present cannot pursue a better historical victory. The more one pursues a better present, the more one can attain a better tomorrow's victory and glory. Recognizing a better self and exposing such a self will only yield opposing results, only the appropriate retribution will come. You must understand this.  
Then what will 1973 be like? You must think about this. A boundary was drawn until 1972, and that time has already come. Regarding this nation and this people, we stand in a position where we can stand. We have reached the boundary where we can have an influence. What will we do from here? You must understand that we are at a point where we must either strike or not, overcome or not.  
Now is truly the time to once again rev up and reach the highest speed. We must apply the strongest force here. To overcome a more innovative environment, I must become an innovative subject. I am the problem, our family is the problem, our church is the problem.  
You do not know the importance of the time. That is why a teacher is needed. If you do not have a conscious awareness of the time, you must march according to the guidance of the teacher. You must march. This is the greatest mission you must undertake in the remaining six months.  
In the historical age, the Unification Church has not yet been liberated from the path of suffering and has gone through an unjust history. You must understand that this period is crucial in determining whether the church can raise the flag of liberation and call for the second and third liberation, and you must resolve to become heirs who can inherit a shining tomorrow from today.  
We must all become a mobilization unit.  
To do this, we must involve heaven. And we must find our conscious selves more deeply and widely and collide there. You must understand this. It is time for the association itself to engage in such activities from now on. You must realize that the time is approaching when we must exert all our capabilities and invest them in one purpose, and we must make a new resolution.  
Moreover, I know that there are many naive people among the mobilization members who know nothing, but we must all become a mobilization unit. The church leaders in Seoul and all the members of the Seoul church must awaken anew. A mobilization unit is not a group that moves based on some plan, right? While deciding whether to live or die, we must present a new revival and a new environment to everyone and create a breakthrough to avoid the sorrows of the losers in tomorrow.  
Therefore, all members of the Unification Church must unite here. There can be no other forms of activity. Churches that have finished gatherings through mobilization activities must carry out mobilization activities centered around their church leaders. The time has come when such activities must be presented as more united and collective than ever.  
When this happens, we can present a nationwide movement. The time has come for that. Hasn't the environment urgently demanded this? In universities, in towns, in cities, across the entire nation, when such activities are presented, depending on how we turn this direction, we can engage in victory activities, church activities, the Saemaul movement, and various fields of activity.  
Thus, how to establish an activity system where the whole can move in unison in this direction is now the most important issue for our Unification Church. We must understand that we are at such a point. Knowing this, the members of the mobilization unit must run at the forefront with a sense of mission and responsibility.  
There is only the will of heaven, only the nation that heaven seeks. There is nothing else. When it comes to God's will, it is not about wanting one’s family to be good. That is not the intention. Such intentions belong to the desires of the animal kingdom. Loving one's offspring is the desire of the animal kingdom. Thinking about one’s parents and relatives, wanting to see them, and thinking about them is something anyone can feel and possess. Even the most inferior creatures have such thoughts.  
Being human means having the authority and value of being the master of all things through overcoming for something greater. Once a man leaves home, can he return with an ugly appearance? If a man draws his sword, he must make a life-and-death decision. With this sword, he must either kill or be killed. You must understand this.  
The Unification Church has faced numerous persecutions until now, but it must not become a Unification Church that can disappear from the stage of persecution. "No matter how fierce the storm may blow, we will advance! The blowing wind may serve as a condition to strengthen my resolve, but it cannot be a condition for retreat." We must burn with this belief. You must understand that you have fought until now with such a belief.  
That is why you must live for heaven. Thirty million people are watching you, and not only that, the entire humanity is watching. You must think that the members in America, Germany, England, and Japan are running shoulder to shoulder with you.  
What is needed is reality over words and results over excuses.  
Mobilization members of Korea, who boast of being the subject nation and the leading nation! Is this how you should be? The ancestors of many countries in the spirit world are comparing and compiling statistics. Isn’t your performance recorded on the situation board every month? When you think of these issues, it is foolish to think only of yourself.  
When a national representative athlete steps onto the starting line on behalf of the nation's fate, that moment is tense, determining not only his own life’s fate but also the fate of the nation. However, if he neglects this and becomes a representative athlete who collapses under the fatigue of his own body, that cannot be allowed. If that happens, nothing will be accomplished. I will only run with the firm belief that I will win, even if I die, and I must achieve victory and collapse. Only running like this, only fighting like this is the duty of athletes who have stepped onto the racecourse. If you do not die, you will surely win... This is all that is required.  
Only then can you become the sons and daughters of God, who is historical, who is historical and also contemporary, and who is contemporary and also future-oriented. Through the past, present, and future, you members of the mobilization unit must not be ashamed before the historical God. You must not become ashamed before this global contemporary era. You must not become ashamed in the future either.  
To do this, my posture must be right. The direction must be right, and the purpose must be right. I must believe in heaven, and by believing in heaven, I must make heaven believe in me. "Please believe in me." You must become the subject. "I will not become a coward. Before I die, I will do this. When faced with danger, I will break through it with death and explode it." Those who have such beliefs must become the mobilization unit.  
Even if I am young and have a shallow history in the Unification Church, I must not be swept away by that shallow history but must step on history and establish a subjective and objective ideology. You must understand that the time is now when it is more strongly required how to establish this.  
When I have the belief that I will serve heaven even if my hands and feet are broken, heaven will be with me. The gaze that looks at me as a witness on behalf of heaven is sharp. No matter how many evil groups block my way and collide head-on, I must burn with the belief that I will break through it and make it shatter. When I step into the street and face people, if there is something opposing, I must think, "Today, a good bait has been caught. A good fish has been caught. It’s a showdown with me!" With such beliefs... If I cannot do it with means, I must step out with wisdom, and if I cannot do it with wisdom, I must step out with strength. I must not lose.  
If I turn back, I must have the belief in my heart that "I did not lose." If I turn back with the sorrowful heart of a loser, I will become a dropout from there. You have not been on this journey for long, but you must move with such a mindset.  
The mobilization unit of the Unification Church, which has been activated by investing funds and providing assistance, is unprecedented in our church's history. This is an unprecedented endeavor in history. Standing in the ranks of such activities is a formidable thing. Looking at you as an individual, you can make one person the responsible leader of a church.  
This time, I plan to support the female members who are out there with one thousand won each month. I am providing two thousand won to special evangelists. This is more than double the support. This is a tremendous expenditure for our church. However, at this critical moment when we can overcome the historical misfortunes, there must be a group that can endure even such endeavors, which is why we are taking risks. We are investing a significant amount of resources.  
We are not providing such support to mobilization members abroad like you. In the United States, in the United Kingdom, and everywhere, they are all solving their own issues. After three months, it will gradually decrease. We must have an independent ideology and carry out the belief of a pioneer independently. Heaven needs such people. One person who leads is needed more than ten people who are being led. That is what is required.  
Today, if we establish a mobilization unit and provide such support behind it, we can certainly create a splendid church in any region, and even if we appoint a leader, we can appoint someone more excellent than anyone else. As you know, if we provide that much support centered around established church pastors, there are countless people on our side who can fight.
You must understand that your responsibility is crucial in engaging in such unprecedented activities. When you step out onto the streets, you should not become a coward who feels ashamed just because someone points a finger at you or a passing friend mocks you. The teacher, even while wearing handcuffs and walking through the streets of Seodaemun, never became a coward. He held the belief that, “Is there anyone who laughs at me for wearing these handcuffs? Yes, you are driving a nail into my heart that cannot be removed. You may treat me with such ridicule, but until the day your descendants bow their heads and kneel before me, who possesses virtue, I cannot die. I cannot refrain from fighting.” He regarded all such materials as the driving force to overcome the living environment. It is not a bad thing. It is not bad to endure humiliation in that regard. “Yes! Today is like this, but who will be the victor tomorrow? I will not stand in the sorrowful position of the loser.” That was his thought. The loser is someone no one sympathizes with.

The Unification Church has left behind historical achievements accompanied by heaven, while pledging to overcome this fateful path of suffering, which is why today we have laid the groundwork for this global foundation. Will you shine and inherit this foundation, or will you retreat in shame and hand it over to others? You must recognize that such questions are approaching you.

What is needed is fact rather than words, results rather than excuses. You all must understand this. Excuses do not work. Words do not matter in front of results. The outcome is severe and cold. If it is right, it concludes as right; if it is bad, it concludes as bad. Victory concludes as victory. The loser concludes with sorrow and misery. You must understand that this is the path of historical judgment.

We must absorb for the purpose of the whole. At this indifferent present moment, do you have the confidence to face your true self and pioneer tomorrow? You must have a self that has undergone self-criticism and awareness; otherwise, it becomes a shame. Acting without being a model for the younger generation is not acceptable. If you want to do that, you might as well retreat altogether.

The reason you are being put out on the streets to engage in such movements is not because there is a desire for you to be worse than you are now. Overcoming one year, two years, three years, when this gradually leads to victorious results, your glory will shine in the world, in history, and you will stand as the center of reality. This is known better than anyone else, which is why such commands are given. To achieve this, you must overcome the difficulties of today, break through the current environment, and pledge the sacrifices of the present. That is the natural principle.

Both cannot be good. One side must yield. So, will you yield the path centered on yourself, or will you allow the overall purpose to be sacrificed? When considering this issue, the self-centered purpose must yield, and you must be absorbed for the sake of the overall purpose. This is the teaching of the principle. You must understand this and now, from the first day of today, how will you overcome the remaining six months, 180 days? You must do well.

Then, what are the men doing at home while the women are out evangelizing? You must think about that. It is not just about eating and lying around. You must know this and feel the new self that can overcome the harsh waves of the current reality, where heaven and your self become one. From here, you must have a subjective belief and be more loyal, more sacrificial, and more invested in yourself. How can you adapt such a self to the whole? Through this issue, you can overcome reality and surpass the historical reality of victory; otherwise, it cannot exist.

Moreover, this must stand out more than the existing historical standards of victory to become the foundation of future hope; otherwise, it will only be a condition for criticism. They say, “What does it matter?” and then it all disappears. The future seeks to inherit the victorious foundation of the present, so you must understand that the future requires a tangible outcome of victory that can be inherited.

From this perspective, when you say “God’s will,” you must understand that it is about saving the world. God has also been mobilized for this reason. God has been mobilized since creation and has not rested for a day, yet I, born as His son or daughter, feel ashamed that I have only now come to participate in this after understanding such things through the historical process. I must yearn in my heart for how to connect with the ties that heaven has been working on throughout history. Regretting not having joined heaven, I must have the belief that I will invest several times more than what I have done in my life’s mission so far. Heaven will recognize such a person as having greater value than the founders of history.

To be able to stand as the center of the present and as the vanguard of the future, and to remain before heaven, I must go out with the belief that I will sacrifice more, not only in the past but also in the present and future. Only in doing so will the results of the purpose centered on you surely improve, and the foundation of that victory will remain in your life and life course.

You must understand these issues well. The present is the problem. Without becoming a better present, there can be no development. If we do not inherit a better present, heaven cannot be with us. Without creating a better present foundation, the future cannot start from a new foundation, can it?

From this perspective, on this first day of July, I hope you will resolutely move forward for the remaining six months, both internally and externally. I will conclude my words here. Do you understand? “Yes.”

<Prayer> Beloved Father, we know that this holy ground is the central holy ground connected to numerous holy sites spread across 40 countries. Every time we stand here, we must inherit not only the heart that thinks of this Korea but also your concern for humanity. Every time we stand here, we recall what you intended to leave behind in the world in 1965 and the sorrowful heart you had for restoration. Thank you for allowing us this time to pledge that we cannot leave behind a foundation for the future unless we become historical victors, not historical losers, gathering the young children here.

Today is July 1st. From the many sorrows of the 1960s to the 1970s, we have spent 12 years and are now entering 1972. Father, please protect us for the next three years. Please manage the fate of this nation.

Our sincerity has been lacking. We have often heard that people from the Unification Church speak well. We must not become those who are criticized for having a big mouth but a narrow heart. Before having a big mouth, we must have a big heart, and we earnestly hope to be your children who can act with a greater goal in mind rather than just for ourselves.

Father, please protect the latter half of 1972. We must go as you lead us. Standing on the Mount of Gethsemane, may we be your children who can inherit the heart of Jesus, who cried out, “Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as you will.” Age does not determine faithfulness, nor does being young prevent one from being faithful.

Father, our hearts are drawn before you. Our hearts long for you. Our hearts are captivated by a heart of admiration before you. We want to go to that place we wish to meet. We want to stand in a position where we can receive commands. No matter how difficult, severe, or miserable those commands may be, the commands received directly from you are the commands that move history, so we must become those who desire to stand in such a serious position.

Father, we have come to know that heaven is not absent but present. We have come to know that there are many people fighting alongside heaven. We know that even when there were no such people, they left behind a history of struggle, and we understand that those who cannot fight even when there are people present are the weak.

Father, when we look at the house we live in, we must not become those who boast about that house. We must not become those who boast about the place we are walking. We must understand that the house we can live in is not that house, and the path we can take is not this path. We must realize that the place where we breathe should not be a place of sorrow but a place where we breathe with the heart of heaven’s concern. We must be your children who can feel that we should breathe and live as the highest victors liberated in the ideal center, in the place of liberation of heaven and earth, in the foundation of the welcome of freedom.

Father, from today, please take charge of this month. Please take charge of this year. As we greet the morning and send off the evening with you, and as we pass on the days and the months, may this year be remembered as a year that cannot be forgotten, a year that can remain in the history of our lives, and may the latter half of 1972 be granted to us.

We see many people who are aging without realizing it, and the youthful era is passing, entering into middle age or old age. If there are those who discover their dwindling strength, Father, let them know better than anyone that impatience is the path of life and the course of restoration.

Father, it is not something to boast about being young. It is not a time to rest. We come to realize that the great waves of restoration’s fate continue to crash upon us, and we cannot rest after overcoming; we must again lead our weary bodies to set out once more on the path of restoration. Heavenly Father, we have come to 1972 without knowing, but now we know that there are still great waves to overcome, and we must not become a pitiful group that retreats at this point.

Now, because our strength is lacking, we must cling to heaven. Just like Jesus prayed, “Father, not my will, but yours be done,” while shedding tears like blood, we know that the time is approaching when we cannot remain without going through the earnest channel of heaven’s circumstances. Please be with us.

We know that there is a Father who gathers the insignificant and directs them along one path. If the steps we are taking on this path become weary, please urge our steps, and if we fall from exhaustion, please spur us on for the sake of tomorrow’s nation, for the sake of tomorrow’s new country… (The rest is not recorded and could not be organized.) 
*
